         <div class="overlappingContent-content-container">
          <h2 class="text text_24 text_36Lg mix-text_primaryFont mix-text_extraBold">
           We are the University of Denver
          </h2>
          <div class="box box_top2 box_top3Md">
           <p class="text text_18 text_20Lg mix-text_secondaryFont mix-text_darkestGray mix-text_lineHeight70">
            University College is proud to be part of a forward-thinking institution and one of 10 colleges at the University of Denver.
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="box box_top1">
           <ul class="blocks blocks_2upDesktop">
            <li>
             <hr class="dividerLine mix-dividerLine_tightBottom"/>
             <p class="text text_16 mix-text_secondaryFont mix-text_lineHeight70">
              Founded in 1864, the University of Denver is the oldest private independent university in the Rocky Mountain region.
             </p>
            </li>
            <li>
             <hr class="dividerLine mix-dividerLine_tightBottom"/>
             <p class="text text_16 mix-text_secondaryFont mix-text_lineHeight70">
              The University of Denver has nationally recognized academic programs, athletics, and research.
             </p>
            </li>
            <li>
             <hr class="dividerLine mix-dividerLine_tightBottom"/>
             <p class="text text_16 mix-text_secondaryFont mix-text_lineHeight70 box_right2Lg">
              DU serves about 12,000 graduate and undergraduate students through 10 different academic colleges, including University College.
             </p>
            </li>
            <li>
             <hr class="dividerLine mix-dividerLine_tightBottom"/>
             <p class="text text_16 mix-text_secondaryFont mix-text_lineHeight70">
              Spread across 125 acres, the University of Denver campus is located about five miles south of downtown Denver.
             </p>
            </li>
           </ul>
          </div>
          <div class="box box_top4">
           <a class="link link_button" href="https://du.edu/about/index.html" target="_blank">
